--**********************************************************************************************************************
-- MEMBER 테이블 삭제
DROP TABLE MEMBER CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
-- MEMBER 테이블 생성
CREATE TABLE MEMBER (
    MNUM NUMBER,
    MEMBER_ID VARCHAR2(20) CONSTRAINT PKID PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
    MEMBER_PWD VARCHAR2(20) CONSTRAINT MPWD NOT NULL,
    MEMBER_NAME VARCHAR2(20) CONSTRAINT MNAME NOT NULL,
    MEMBER_EMAIL VARCHAR2(20) CONSTRAINT MEMAIL NOT NULL,
    EMAILAUTH VARCHAR2(20) CONSTRAINT MAUTH NOT NULL,
    MEMBER_PHONE VARCHAR2(15) CONSTRAINT MPHONE NOT NULL,
    JOIN_DATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
    LAST_ACCESS_DATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
   SECESSION_OK CHAR(1)   DEFAULT 'Y'   CONSTRAINT SS_OK NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT CHK_SES CHECK (SECESSION_OK IN ('Y','N')),
    SECESSION_DATE DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE
);

-- MEMBER 컬럼명
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MNUM IS '번호';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MEMBER_ID IS '회원 아이디';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MEMBER_PWD IS '회원 패스워드';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MEMBER_NAME IS '회원 이름';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MEMBER_EMAIL IS '회원 이메일';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.EMAILAUTH IS '이메일인증';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.MEMBER_PHONE IS '회원 전화번호';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.JOIN_DATE IS '가입일';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.LAST_ACCESS_DATE IS '최근접속일';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.SECESSION_OK IS '탈퇴여부';
COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.SECESSION_DATE IS '탈퇴일';

DROP TABLE "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" cascade constraints;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table LOCATION
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" 
   (	"LOCAL_NO" VARCHAR2(3 BYTE), 
	"LOCAL_NAME" VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	"KMAP_Y" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"KMAP_X" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE)
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" ;

   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."LOCATION"."LOCAL_NO" IS '지역번호';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."LOCATION"."LOCAL_NAME" IS '지역이름(구)';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."LOCATION"."KMAP_Y" IS '지역별 중심 위치 위도';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."LOCATION"."KMAP_X" IS '지역별 중심 위치 경도';

  CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "ANAVADA"."PK_LOCAL_NO" ON "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" ("LOCAL_NO") 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  Constraints for Table LOCATION
--------------------------------------------------------

  ALTER TABLE "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" ADD CONSTRAINT "PK_LOCAL_NO" PRIMARY KEY ("LOCAL_NO")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM"  ENABLE;
  ALTER TABLE "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" MODIFY ("LOCAL_NAME" NOT NULL ENABLE);
  ALTER TABLE "ANAVADA"."LOCATION" MODIFY ("LOCAL_NO" NOT NULL ENABLE);

--  DDL for Table FBOARD

  CREATE TABLE "ANAVADA"."FBOARD" 
   (	"FBOARD_NO" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"FESTIVAL_TITLE" VARCHAR2(600 BYTE), 
	"LOCAL_NO" VARCHAR2(3 BYTE), 
	"FESTIVAL_STARTDATE" VARCHAR2(8 BYTE), 
	"FESTIVAL_ENDDATE" VARCHAR2(8 BYTE), 
	"FESTIVAL_MODIFIEDDATE" VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	"MAP_Y" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"MAP_X" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"BMODIFY_DATE" DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE, 
	"MEMBER_ID" VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	"READCOUNT" NUMBER DEFAULT 0, 
	"THUMBNAIL" VARCHAR2(100 BYTE) DEFAULT 'NoImage'
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" ;

   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."FBOARD_NO" IS '축제게시판 번호';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."FESTIVAL_TITLE" IS '축제 이름';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."LOCAL_NO" IS '지역 번호';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."FESTIVAL_STARTDATE" IS '축제 시작일';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."FESTIVAL_ENDDATE" IS '축제 종료일';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."FESTIVAL_MODIFIEDDATE" IS '축제 수정일';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."MAP_Y" IS '축제 위도';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."MAP_X" IS '축제 경도';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."BMODIFY_DATE" IS '축제게시판 수정일';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."MEMBER_ID" IS '작성자';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."READCOUNT" IS '조회수';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "ANAVADA"."FBOARD"."THUMBNAIL" IS '썸네일';
